<review>My order: Chicken Veggie, More Veggie(which means less rice), and Brown Rice.
Always delicious and always affordable!
I did notice they are hoarding the enjoyable teriyaki sauce now... Which is a shame because I would take about a dozen and save it for later...don't judge me until you've tasted its glory.

Not a lot of outdoor seating and they do share a location with Stans Donuts. Goodluck trying to ignore the amazing aroma of fried dough....yummmm

< review>
(Translated by Google) I got into a parking war and barely got my car in the meter and came in hungry. It's owned by a Korean woman, but I knew it was a butcher shop. I had an AK Decadence sandwich and a meatball sandwich for $ 7.50 each. If you have two tables at the entrance, it's good to eat in the sun. Compared to Subway Turkey Sandwich, it's about $ 3 more expensive. Turkey ham contains a lot, avocado tends to taste smoothly, and vegetables have fresh young sprouts. I also had some meatballs at other American sandwich shops, but it was delicious because I had meatballs in Korea.

< Text>
There are several dining halls in Berkeley, but Foothill is my favorite. This is my first semester in Stern and I live in a girl‚Äôs dorm, needless to say, I have to find a place where I can eat good, healthy and not so expensive food in order to survive! Foothill is placed conveniently close to where I currently live, so it‚Äôs my favorite and closest place for having dinner or late night snack when I miss the dinner. They are serving dinner from 5pm to 8pm and it is more like all you can eat buffet. The menu is not always the same and that is what I like about it, there is always something new and unique on the menu and so far everything I tried was delicious as heck! They post their menu online every day so you can easily take a sneak-peek at what you will be having for dinner. ¬†My fave is the tri tip with chimichurri sauce. The food is fresh and they also have a decent choice for vegetarians.< /Text>

Great store for Indian groceries, spices, kitchenware, etc. The people are so nice and helpful. They have fresh produce, the normal stuff and some specialty type of ingredients like kafir lime leaves, Indian bitter melon, chilies, etc. It's a big warehouse type market and is fun to walk around and look at all the interesting products. <Rating>5</Rating>< review>
Santos Spice Products is a wonderful resource for San Leandro, San Lorenzo, Oakland, and Hayward. Great selection, from fresh produce and dairy, to dry foods. I'm not at all well studied in the cultures and cooking of South Asia, but to my inexperienced eye it looks to me like there are foods and flavors for a whole subcontinent to be found on the shelves. I went looking for frozen gandules (pigeon peas) for use in arroz con gandules Puerto Rican style, and there were plenty in stock. Also needed some paneer, and was delighted to find a package made from organic milk. Got a few spices, and a snack mix - the place made my mouth water. While checking out, I admired the housewares. If you're looking for a good place with helpful and knowledgeable staff, go to Santos Spice Products, your pallet will thank you.< /review>

I'm so happy they are here in San Leandro. The price/value is amazing. I don't think I could get it cheaper anywhere else near here.

There's also a refrigerated section where you can get frozen Indian food or just normal veggies. I can highly recommend their plain yogurt and naans as well. The most alluring is probably the counter itself. There are loads of sweets, pastries and other baked goods (again... samosas!).

A cozy little tea house with a quaint, homey vibe to it. Like many shops in the area, it attracts a young, hip, college crowd. There is a large selection of hand mixed, loose-leaf teas. Each tea that I've tried (about 6) is wonderful, and really hits the spot on cold nights. The only real complaint that I have is that some of the staff, particularly the older gentleman, is impatient and a bit rude. < Review>
Platinum Collision Repair exceeded my expectations which is hard to do. PCC provided me a level of customer service from like the good old days when life was so much more simpler. From my first call I was treated like a V.I.P. They had their own tow service pick up my Model S Tesla promptly and from there on it was like I was staying at a 5 star hotel. When I arrived  I walked through the service stalls to the reception...backwards through a shop really. Most companies today due to liabilities would not allow a customer to walk through its shop floor. Anyway, the shop was so  extra clean you could practically eat off the floor. When we made it to the receptionist at the front of the building I was offered refreshments, water soda, coffee...really! I was then introduced to Crystal, my personal service support staff.
In the four weeks I worked with Crystal it was like being the CEO of a large company and she was my personal administrative assistant. Crystal handled every detail from working with Tesla Corporation for parts to my insurance company over budgets. She was always one step a head of me in communicating repair  status.
Check this out.  My insurance budgeted for used parts since my car was nearly six years old. PCC charged my insurance company only for used parts, but installed new OEM parts for me at the same price!
When I picked up the car (BTW mintly detailed to perfection) I got a walk around from Jan, one of the managers. Honestly, he gave me the time and attention as if I was part of his family. He showed me pictures on his cell phone on the progress of the repairs to my car! You would have thought it was his car not mine!! He took the time to educate me on all the meticulous details that went into fixing my ‚ÄúBaby.‚Äù I so appreciated the education and the special attention. Thank you Jan and Crystal and for the entire PCC staff for an amazing, headache free experience.
To future customers, you shouldn‚Äôt be surprised at this level of service however...There was a new Bentley being towed in right behind my car!
This is my first ever post for any company. As a business owner myself my hats off to PCC for an exceptional business model.< /Review>

<Text>The service, professionalism and care at Platinum Collision Center were all superb.  The entire staff, from the receptionist to the owner (Tom), consistently provided excellent service beyond my expectations.

I had a minor fender-bender on my Tesla and needed to have the rear bumper repaired.
The estimate process was quick and easy.  Jackie meets you at the front desk in the most friendly and helpful manner.  Veronica assesses the damage thoroughly and provides the estimate.  They set up an immediate date for my repair and even made arrangements for me to get  a rental car at the site.  All I had to do was drop off my car.

Jhann, the manager, keeps you informed about the entire repair process.  He is very knowledgeable and experienced.  He works with the insurance company to get the repairs covered and completed as quickly as possible.  When my insurance company, State Farm, became less than willing to cover the necessary repairs, Jhann effectively communicated with me and State Farm to explain each itemized cost.  In the end, all repairs were beautifully done and covered with a lifetime warranty.

I am extremely satisfied with my experience at Platinum.   Thank you for the excellent service.  I highly recommend Platinum Collision Center in Eastvale!< /Text><Pictures>None</Pictures>< response>

The food is really good! Service sucks. First time was a very simple to go order, just one plate. I went inside to get it too, it wasn't curbside. There was no one in line behind me, yet the young white girl that rang me up stood her ground and stared at me while I put away my wallet, as if she expected a tip? I could have been wrong but that's what I felt from her, which was annoying. I don't usually tip for to go orders, only eat in, unless it was a complicated order that was prepared and packed correctly.
The reason I'm not too thrilled with this place was because of my next visit a few months after that. It took my family of 4 about 2.5 hours to get through dinner. We had a reservation and got there on time, yet they gave away our table? We waited about 7 minutes in the crowded waiting area and were only seated because a table opened up and we weren't gonna be stiffed since we had a reservation.
It was a busy Mother's Day granted, but still shouldn't take an hour to get our appetizer.... We asked where our app was after about 20 minutes. Obvious our waitress forgot (some young white girl, maybe the same one as before, IDK). She said we didn't order it but she'll go put in the order. 20ish minutes after that, we ask again where it is, she comes back and claims the ovens were down?? We look around and see that other people were enjoying the same app so we called BS and asked again. A few minutes later lo and behold here she comes with our app. Afterwards while ordering our entrees, I asked what a particular pasta dish on the menu was like, so I can explain it to my mom who only understands spanish. After ordering, we asked for a manager to complain and for a new server. New server was Hispanic and polite, smooth sailing after that. Entrees and dessert took a while as well but whatever it's a holiday, and our server kept us posted and checked up on us and our drinks. Super respectful and professional. Nice tip for her.</Review>

< Text>
I've been coming to Macaroni Grill for at least 10 years, we love coming here and are sad when they change up their menu, because we just get so use to ordering the same things that it usually become our favorite dish, and then they discontinue making it. Anyhow, last Wednesday evening my wife and I met a friend for happy hour at the City of Industry location, and I'm sorry to say that we had the worse experience ever. We sat in the bar, which was a big mistake, the bartender (ex-chola full of attitude) ignored us for at least 15 minutes before we actually walked up to the bar to order a drink and get her attention. We finally get our drinks, and the drinks were terrible, I hate to complain about my food or drinks at bars or restaurants because I don't like to offend anyone, but I just had to send the drink back, it was un-drinkable. I had the bartender make the drink again, and the new drink was just as bad, I just took a sip and just left it. We thought we'd try their new promotion where you order your meal for $9 in 9 min or else it's free... They took 45 minutes to bring us our food and never even came over to check on us, I mean "REALLY" the bar wasn't even full, I'd say there was about 3 tables out of maybe 10 that were being used. Finally, the manager came over and apologized and comped our food, and would you know, that after they cleared our table, and we were ready to pay, the same bartender still took about another 15 min to come over ask me if I needed change, I was like "I still haven't paid, no one has come over to take my card!". No matter how bad the service and experience was, I still tipped her. I probably wont be back to this location for a while, but when I do decide to come back for dinner or a drink and if this same bartender is working the bar, I am just walking right out of there and taking my business else where.</Text>

Its been a nice hot minute since Ive been back to Macaroni Grill, I often the location in Arcadia until they closed down. Now after years, we decided to come back for some last minute hunger fix in the City of Industry area.

They changed up their menu a little bit and have some pretty decent deals. You can order to appetizers for only $9.95 and I'll tell you now..you'll be full from the delicious bread before your entree even shows up.

We had some pretty delicious drinks, bilini cocktail and a blood orange cosmo, they didn't give us "blood orange" and replaced it with just a normal orange so that was misrepresented, but thats it!< /review>
